  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_11f3d7c3-abcc-45d6-b408-7da92e4e328c'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer11798298955201018508">Ido Barnea, an Israeli combat pilot, is flying a routine night flight over the Negev desert when suddenly his reliable Skyhawk jet fighter starts to vibrate uncontrollably and finally crashes, forcing Ido to eject at the last possible second. At that exact moment, in the heart of Brussels, a young girl is kidnapped. What is the connection between those two incidents? Who i</span>
  <span id="freeText11798298955201018508" style="display:none">Ido Barnea, an Israeli combat pilot, is flying a routine night flight over the Negev desert when suddenly his reliable Skyhawk jet fighter starts to vibrate uncontrollably and finally crashes, forcing Ido to eject at the last possible second. At that exact moment, in the heart of Brussels, a young girl is kidnapped. What is the connection between those two incidents? Who is behind them? Accused of betrayal, Ido is forced into a fast-paced dizzying chase in order to clear his name. Naama Sharon, a beautiful Mossad agent is sent after him, and the two encounter powerful arms dealers, cynical terrorists and corrupt army officers. In their struggle, they discover that the two mysterious incidents hide a deplorable crime. The Eagle's Secret is an original, thrilling novel, full of jet-fighter-like twists and turns. Its fast pace will leave you breathless... yet wishing for more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11798298955201018508" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6357685367817567871">The Eagle's Secret is a military thriller full of excitement, speeding planes, crime, killers, and kidnappings that will keep the reader on edge. The protagonist, Ido Barnea, is a pilot who nearly dies in a plane that goes out of control. He knows planes and that something has been tampered with in the plane that crashes after he ejects. He is determined to find out who and what endangered his life. He meets a woman, Naama, who plays an important role in saving his life on more than one occasion</span>
  <span id="freeText6357685367817567871" style="display:none">The Eagle's Secret is a military thriller full of excitement, speeding planes, crime, killers, and kidnappings that will keep the reader on edge. The protagonist, Ido Barnea, is a pilot who nearly dies in a plane that goes out of control. He knows planes and that something has been tampered with in the plane that crashes after he ejects. He is determined to find out who and what endangered his life. He meets a woman, Naama, who plays an important role in saving his life on more than one occasion. Who is she and what part does she play in this mystery of the plane crash?<br /><br />This was an enjoyable book 1 read of a series. The author uses his expertise as a pilot himself to color the story with exciting detail.<br /><br /> </span>

<div id="review_1527698120" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1527698120" />
    <a title="Jacqueline Wagenstein" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15562851-jacqueline-wagenstein"><img alt="Jacqueline Wagenstein" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1355763807p2/15562851.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1527698120?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline Wagenstein" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline Wagenstein" href="/user/show/15562851-jacqueline-wagenstein">Jacqueline Wagenstein</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9786191506217" href="/book/show/28787339">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15562851-jacqueline-wagenstein?shelf=colibri-crime-thrillers">colibri-crime-thrillers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1527698120" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13468276872904230757">Ерез Ахарони е един от най-видните израелски адвокати в областта на търговското право, съдебните дела и недвижимите имоти. Бил е пилот в израелските военновъздушни сили през 1978 г. и е участвал в разнообразни полети и мисии, включително свързани с имиграцията на евреите от Етиопия. Страстта му към литературата го съпровожда още от най-ранна възраст. Дебютният му роман се нарича „Half a Moustache”, излиза през 2006 г. и постига завиден успех. Три години след това се появява военният трилър „Тайн</span>
  <span id="freeText13468276872904230757" style="display:none">Ерез Ахарони е един от най-видните израелски адвокати в областта на търговското право, съдебните дела и недвижимите имоти. Бил е пилот в израелските военновъздушни сили през 1978 г. и е участвал в разнообразни полети и мисии, включително свързани с имиграцията на евреите от Етиопия. Страстта му към литературата го съпровожда още от най-ранна възраст. Дебютният му роман се нарича „Half a Moustache”, излиза през 2006 г. и постига завиден успех. Три години след това се появява военният трилър „Тайната на Орела”. <br /><br />Интригата тук е ще успеят ли терористите да поемат контрол върху израелските изтребители и да унищожат Израел. Изкупителната жертва се казва Идо Барнеа, той е най-новият пилот в ескадрилата. Считат го за своенравен интроверт със състезателен дух, творческо мислене и склонност към морални дебати. От първия му ден в армията са минали над шест години и компромисите със съвестта му идват в повече. И е то че напуска ескадрилата от изтребители F-16, наречена „Рицарите на оранжевата опашка“, защото не иска да изпълнява бойни мисии. <br /><br />В очакване на разрешително за отпуск, Идо управлява самолет с прозвище Орел, скайхоук ветеран, който никога не е причинявал неприятности. Изстрелва светлинни ракети в пустинята Негев. По време на един нощен полет иначе надеждният изтребител го предава, Идо е принуден да катапултира и оцелява като по чудо, а машината се разбива в покрайнините на Беер Шева.<br /><br />Цяло ято герои се втурва по следите на Барнеа, всеки със собствен мотив. По същото време в Брюксел е отвлечено малолетно момиче на име Мишел. Възможно ли е да има връзка между двете събития? В роман на Ерез Ахарони всичко е възможно - броят на „лошите” расте със скоростта на светлината, броят на невинните жертви също. Първо се оказва, че един бедуин е тежко ранен вследствие от катастрофата в пустинята. После умира фотограф, приятел на семейството на Идо. Един от механиците го светва, че преди фаталния полет в самолета е направена някаква нелегална модификация, а на негово място всъщност е трябвало да лети някой друг. Появява се и тайнствена красавица на име Наама Шарон, която по-късно се оказва разузнавачка от „Мосад”. Гледните точки се редуват, което допринася за динамиката на сюжета.<br /><br />Сега целият свят търсеше Идо, а тя не можеше да помогне с нищо. Беше по-добре да се съсредоточи върху задачата да открие кой работи с него. Опита се да насочи мислите си в правилната посока, но въпросите продължаваха да я измъчват. Дали Ярив Сиди наистина беше убит от Идо Барнеа? И ако да – защо? Кой беше изпратил на Идо толкова много пари? И за какво? Дали информацията на Кох е достатъчно точна, за да открие истината? И какво всъщност щеше да прави тя в Белгия с това име и адреса? Толкова много въпроси - толкова малко отговори.<br /><br />Дали Барнеа ще изпревари змията, опитала се да унищожи ръководството на Военновъздушните сили, както и него самия? Способен ли е Барнеа на хладнокръвно, садистично убийство? В състояние ли е един опитен пилот да неутрализира смъртоносна компютърна програма с едно преобръщане във въздуха? Може би, особено ако летенето е онова, което му се удава най-добре. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13468276872904230757" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">
          

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1527698120">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1337344844" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11180024624136622608">This was an enjoyable thriller that moved along at a good pace. Whilst it could be described as formulaic – standard premise of unjustly accused hero who battles against the odds who falls in love with the main protagonist sent to capture him as he strives to clear his name and save the day - it is none the worst for this.<br/> I liked the main characters even if some of actions carried out by them were in the ‘unbelievable’ end of the spectrum. The action scenes were well done and there was just eno</span>
  <span id="freeText11180024624136622608" style="display:none">This was an enjoyable thriller that moved along at a good pace. Whilst it could be described as formulaic – standard premise of unjustly accused hero who battles against the odds who falls in love with the main protagonist sent to capture him as he strives to clear his name and save the day - it is none the worst for this.<br /> I liked the main characters even if some of actions carried out by them were in the ‘unbelievable’ end of the spectrum. The action scenes were well done and there was just enough detail about Mayor ‘vice’ for the reader to understand why he was being blackmailed the author did not descend to unnecessary descriptions which would not have added to the novel.<br /> For me I am always trying to think ‘would I read this author again?’ and here I am undecided. There was nothing in it that makes me want to rush out and read other one of his books, but at the same time I wouldn’t refuse the opportunity to do so if it came it about</span>
  <a data-text-id="11180024624136622608" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1776006534092150990">Another great book from a brilliant mind! I have read other books from this author and have been greatly impressed by the unique writing and excellent plots. Once again, Erez Aharoni brings us a book that is more difficult to put down than the last. If you haven't read the any of the other books by this author, I would suggest to check out "Half a Moustache" "The Eagle's Secret" and "Wildfire".<br/><br/>This man has some excellent international experience and it really shows in his writing. The characters</span>
  <span id="freeText1776006534092150990" style="display:none">Another great book from a brilliant mind! I have read other books from this author and have been greatly impressed by the unique writing and excellent plots. Once again, Erez Aharoni brings us a book that is more difficult to put down than the last. If you haven't read the any of the other books by this author, I would suggest to check out "Half a Moustache" "The Eagle's Secret" and "Wildfire".<br /><br />This man has some excellent international experience and it really shows in his writing. The characters really come to life. I love mystery and thrillers, this book brings those two genres together and makes you think you are in the story.<br /><br />Kidnapping is always a fear in the back of our minds as parents. Reading about kidnapping just hits home, it really makes you have feelings for these characters. Excellent read!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1776006534092150990" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rNH7ETSQJv20w+CnRRc2mBdmiZ/BWPrIDnvOi5mVY8trLaH0UjUAO8z8qTU6WhQ4Tn2ZkL8ek3qQERiYWoUQ9w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rSFGAdNx75tbXsM9hNgVZVZgv1Emmy1k1QjDuyCoRqhq3RzktdTJXSNhiq/7lTfFD3uvXljdRNZLYhWo47g1lA==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer5567976599126948791">Mr. Erez Aharoni grew up in Ramat Gan, Israel. As a child, he led in the boy scouts and played sports. He was drafted to the Israel Air Force, and completed his fighter pilot training course in 1978.<br/><br/>Later on, he served as a pilot in the Hercules squadron, and participated in various flights and missions, including the immigration of the Jews of Ethiopia.<br/><br/>After his discharge, he studied Law, finishi</span>
  <span id="freeText5567976599126948791" style="display:none">Mr. Erez Aharoni grew up in Ramat Gan, Israel. As a child, he led in the boy scouts and played sports. He was drafted to the Israel Air Force, and completed his fighter pilot training course in 1978.<br /><br />Later on, he served as a pilot in the Hercules squadron, and participated in various flights and missions, including the immigration of the Jews of Ethiopia.<br /><br />After his discharge, he studied Law, finishing his degree at Tel Aviv University.<br /><br />Mr. Erez Aharoni is one of Israel's foremost commercial lawyers and one of the founders and managing partner of the international law firm of Zysman, Aharoni, Gayer &amp; Co. Mr. Aharoni is also a partner and an owner of the U.S. law firm ZAG/S&amp;W and of the chinese law firm ZAG/JunZeJun.<br />Mr. Aharoni has gained prominence in the fields of commercial law, litigation, and real estate. Mr. Aharoni specializes in handling the various legal aspects of complex commercial transactions, and has extensive experience in large-scale real estate transactions on a domestic and international basis. He is also an expert on legal and commercial aspects of media and communications law in Israel, and has significant experience in a wide variety of legal issues involving civil and commercial litigation, as well as in legal action in the various judicial instances. Mr. Aharoni has served as liquidator and trustee of large corporations, on behalf of institutional investors, as well as an appointed officer of the court for these purposes.<br /><br />His love of writing and fiction began at a young age. In 2004, his story 'Cackling (The Sounds of the Duck)' won first prize in the Uriel Ofek Short Fiction competition. In 2006, his first book, 'Half a Moustache', was published by Maariv, and three years later, his novel 'The Eagle's Secret' was published by Kinneret Zmora-Bitan.<br /><br />In 2011, his newest book, 'Wildfire', edited by Amnon Jackont, was published by Kinneret Zmora-Bitan.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5567976599126948791" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
